     ├ù POST /api/v1/submissions returns 404 for invalid assignment_id 1465ms
     ├ù POST /api/v1/submissions returns 404 for invalid student_id 1133ms
     ├ù PATCH /api/v1/submissions/:id updates submission score and auto-sets graded_at 1279ms
     ├ù PATCH /api/v1/submissions/:id updates submission comments 1482ms
     ├ù DELETE /api/v1/submissions/:id deletes a submission 1508ms
